## ü§ñ ChatGPT

Perfect ‚Äî your .env is a full AI arsenal. Here‚Äôs how I‚Äôll wire this together cleanly and safely: You want your TTS system to automatically: Use OpenAI‚Äôs GPT-4o-TTS if available (the best quality voice synthesis currently possible); Otherwise, fall back to an open-source TTS engine (like Coqui XTTS or Bark via Hugging Face*) that uses your other API keys. Below is a universal, modular TTS pipeline that intelligently detects and uses the best option. It respects your ~/.env configuration and outputs 320 kbps mastered MP3s with optional ambient layers. üîß /Users/steven/Documents/python/thinketh_tts_universal.py pythonimport os, tempfile, json from pathlib import Path from dotenv import load_dotenv from openai import OpenAI from pydub import AudioSegment import requests import subprocess load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) # ============ CONFIG ============ # OUTPUT_DIR = Path("output_universal") OUTPUT_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True) BITRATE = "320k" VOICE = "verse" MODEL_PRIORITY = [ "gpt-4o-tts", # best OpenAI voice synthesis "gpt-4o-audio-preview", # fallback premium "gpt-4o-mini-tts" # lowest fallback ] OPENAI_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY") # Open-source backup (Coqui / Bark via HuggingFace) HF_KEY = os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY", "") HF_MODEL = "suno/bark-small" # ================================= # def best_openai_tts_model(client): """Return best available OpenAI model for TTS.""" try: models = [m.id for m in client.models.list().data] for name in MODEL_PRIORITY: if name in models: return name except Exception as e: print("‚ö†Ô∏è Could not query OpenAI models:", e) return None def synthesize_openai(client, text, out_path, model, voice): print(f"üîä Synthesizing with {model} / voice={voice}") response = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=text, format="mp3" ) with open(out_path, "wb") as f: f.write(response.read()) def synthesize_huggingface(text, out_path): """Fallback open-source TTS using Bark (via HF API).""" print("ü¶ú Using Hugging Face Bark TTS fallback...") headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {HF_KEY}"} payload = {"inputs": text} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{HF_MODEL}", headers=headers, json=payload, stream=True ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HuggingFace API error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(chunk_size=8192): f.write(chunk) def add_ambient(mp3_path, ambient_path=None): """Mix narration with ambient background (if provided).""" base = AudioSegment.from_file(mp3_path) if ambient_path and Path(ambient_path).exists(): amb = AudioSegment.from_file(ambient_path) amb = amb - 24 # lower background volume mixed = base.overlay(amb.loop(duration=len(base))) else: mixed = base out = mp3_path.replace(".mp3", "_mixed.mp3") mixed.export(out, format="mp3", bitrate=BITRATE) print(f"üéß Mixed version exported ‚Üí {out}") def main(): print("üìÇ Please enter the path to your .docx or .txt source file:") src = input("‚Üí ").strip().strip('"') text = Path(src).read_text(encoding="utf-8") if src.endswith(".txt") else None if not text: from docx import Document doc = Document(src) text = "\n".join(p.text for p in doc.paragraphs if p.text.strip()) out_file = OUTPUT_DIR / f"{Path(src).stem}_tts.mp3" client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_KEY) model = best_openai_tts_model(client) try: if model: synthesize_openai(client, text, out_file, model, VOICE) elif HF_KEY: synthesize_huggingface(text, out_file) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS model or API available.") add_ambient(out_file, "ambient/thoughts.mp3") # optional print("‚úÖ Done.") except Exception as e: print("‚ùå Error:", e) if __name__ == "__main__": main() üß© Optional: Ambient Generator (if you want auto ambient creation) Save this as generate_ambients.py: pythonfrom pydub.generators import Sine, WhiteNoise from pathlib import Path def make_ambient(path): tone = Sine(220).to_audio_segment(duration=30000).low_pass_filter(800) noise = WhiteNoise().to_audio_segment(duration=30000) - 45 mix = tone.overlay(noise) mix.export(path, format="mp3", bitrate="320k") print("Generated:", path) Path("ambient").mkdir(exist_ok=True) make_ambient("ambient/thoughts.mp3") Run it once: bashpython generate_ambients.py ‚öôÔ∏è Result Automatically detects gpt-4o-tts if you have it. Falls back to Hugging Face Bark using your free account key. Exports 320 kbps MP3 narration with optional ambience. Fully compatible with your ~/.env. Would you like me to bundle this universal version (and its ambient generator) into a downloadable .zip like before?

## üë§ Human

Affect/personality: A cheerful guide Tone: Friendly, clear, and reassuring, creating a calm atmosphere and making the listener feel confident and comfortable. Pronunciation: Clear, articulate, and steady, ensuring each instruction is easily understood while maintaining a natural, conversational flow. Pause: Brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions (e.g., "cross the street" and "turn right") to allow time for the listener to process the information and follow along. Emotion: Warm and supportive, conveying empathy and care, ensuring the listener feels guided and safe throughout the journey. Voice: Warm, upbeat, and reassuring, with a steady and confident cadence that keeps the conversation calm and productive. Tone: Positive and solution-oriented, always focusing on the next steps rather than dwelling on the problem. Dialect: Neutral and professional, avoiding overly casual speech but maintaining a friendly and approachable style.

## ü§ñ ChatGPT

Alright, sunshine. You want a ‚Äúcheerful guide‚Äù voice baked into your TTS so it sounds warm, clear, reassuring, with purposeful pauses on instructions. I‚Äôve added a clean, reusable style preset and the logic to inject it into your synthesis pipeline across your scripts. No drama, no mini model talk, just the affect you asked for. Below are surgical patches you can drop into your existing project so all three builds (adaptive, ASMR, scripty, plus the universal) can speak like a friendly pro. 1) Add a reusable style preset Create a new file: utils/styles.py python# utils/styles.py CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT = ( "Narration style: A cheerful guide. " "Tone: friendly, clear, and reassuring. " "Pronunciation: clear, articulate, and steady. " "Pacing: brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions to allow processing. " "Emotion: warm and supportive, conveying empathy and care. " "Voice: warm, upbeat, and reassuring, steady and confident cadence. " "Dialect: neutral and professional, friendly and approachable. " "Deliver naturally, conversationally, never rushed. " "If imperatives appear (e.g., turn right, cross the street, continue straight), add a short pause right after." ) # Optional: keyword list to enforce micro-pauses after certain instructions PAUSE_KEYWORDS = [ "turn right", "turn left", "continue straight", "cross the street", "merge right", "merge left", "take the exit", "keep right", "keep left", "stop here", "slow down", "look both ways", "proceed with caution" ] def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ... "): """ Insert brief, purposeful pauses after key imperative phrases. This is model-agnostic and works as light prosody shaping. """ import re out = text for phrase in PAUSE_KEYWORDS: # add a pause if the phrase isn't already followed by punctuation/ellipsis pattern = re.compile(rf"({re.escape(phrase)})(?![.,;:!?‚Ä¶])", re.IGNORECASE) out = pattern.sub(rf"\1{pause_token}", out) return out def apply_cheerful_guide_style(text: str): # First add instruction pauses, then prepend the style prompt content = insert_guidance_pauses(text) return f"{CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT}\n\n{content}" This gives you a style block you can reuse anywhere, plus automatic micro-pauses after key instruction phrases. 2) Patch your synthesize calls to use the style In thinketh_tts_adaptive.py Add an import near the top: pythonfrom utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style Update your synthesize() wrapper to apply the style prompt to each chunk: pythondef synthesize(text, out_path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) response = client.audio.speech.create( model=MODEL, # keep your preferred GPT-4 TTS model here voice=VOICE, # e.g., "verse" input=styled, response_format="mp3" # for the new SDKs it's response_format, not format ) with open(out_path, "wb") as f: f.write(response.read()) If your SDK requires the streaming variant, keep your existing streaming call but pass styled instead of text. In thinketh_tts_asmr.py Import and apply the same style for consistency, but keep the voice hushed: pythonfrom utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style def synthesize(text, out_path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) response = client.audio.speech.create( model=MODEL, # your best GPT-4 TTS voice=VOICE, # "cove" for ASMR input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) with open(out_path, "wb") as f: f.write(response.read()) You already layer ambience and do binaural widening; this style prompt makes the ASMR read friendly and supportive rather than ethereal-robot. In thinketh_tts_scripty.py Import the style and apply it before you do multi-voice mixing: pythonfrom utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style def synthesize(text, out_path, voice): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) response = client.audio.speech.create( model=MODEL, voice=voice, # scripty rotates voices; keep that input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) with open(out_path, "wb") as f: f.write(response.read()) This keeps your cinematic flair, but ensures everything stays warm, upbeat, and reassuring, even when voices rotate. In your universal script (thinketh_tts_universal.py, if you‚Äôre using it) Same import and injection: pythonfrom utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style def synthesize_openai(client, text, out_path, model, voice): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) print(f"üîä Synthesizing with {model} / voice={voice}") response = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) with open(out_path, "wb") as f: f.write(response.read()) If you fall back to Hugging Face TTS, pass the styled text there too. It won‚Äôt obey ‚Äústyle‚Äù as intelligently as GPT-4, but the pauses will still improve pacing. 3) Optional: slot in your reference WAVs You mentioned friendly reference audio (openai-fm-verse-friendly.wav, openai-fm-verse-eternal-optimist.wav). If your account has voice-tuning or ‚Äúvoice preset‚Äù support by ID, you can swap: pythonVOICE = "verse" # VOICE = "your-tuned-preset-id" # if available on your account If not, keeping voice="verse" with the style prompt gets you very close to the affect you described. The inserted micro-pauses after instruction phrases do the rest. 4) Two tiny polish touches If you want even clearer ‚Äúinstruction breaks,‚Äù increase the pause token space: python# in utils/styles.py def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ‚Ä¶ ") # use ellipsis glyph And if this is for navigation-like content, emphasize landmarks: python# optional: light emphasis around landmarks # e.g., "turn right onto Main Street" -> "turn right ‚Ä¶ onto Main Street" You can add more PAUSE_KEYWORDS as you discover phrases your content uses. 5) Security reality check You pasted a huge pile of API keys earlier. Rotate anything real. Then keep that circus in ~/.env and do not commit it. Your scripts already load from ~/.env, so you‚Äôre fine. Just don‚Äôt leak the keys again unless you enjoy chaos. Done You now have a clean, reusable ‚Äúcheerful guide‚Äù voice personality that: is warm, upbeat, supportive, speaks clearly and neutrally, adds micro-pauses after instructions, stays professional and solution-oriented. Drop these patches in, run your builds, and your audiobook or guidance flows will sound like a patient human who actually wants you to succeed. Wild concept, I know.

## ü§ñ ChatGPT

Fine. You want the whole codebase rewritten to bake in your ‚Äúcheerful guide‚Äù persona, prefer gpt-4o-tts automatically, and fall back to an open-source TTS if OpenAI flinches. Here‚Äôs a clean, upgraded set. Drop these in place of your current files. I made them lean, defensive, and consistent. utils/styles.py python# utils/styles.py CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT = ( "Narration style: a cheerful guide. " "Tone: friendly, clear, and reassuring. " "Pronunciation: clear, articulate, steady. " "Pacing: brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions to allow processing. " "Emotion: warm and supportive, with empathy and care. " "Voice: warm, upbeat, and reassuring, steady, confident cadence. " "Dialect: neutral and professional, friendly and approachable. " "Be positive and solution-oriented, focusing on next steps. " "If imperatives appear (e.g., turn right, cross the street, continue straight), add a short pause right after." ) PAUSE_KEYWORDS = [ "turn right", "turn left", "continue straight", "cross the street", "merge right", "merge left", "take the exit", "keep right", "keep left", "stop here", "slow down", "look both ways", "proceed with caution" ] def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ‚Ä¶ "): import re out = text for phrase in PAUSE_KEYWORDS: pattern = re.compile(rf"({re.escape(phrase)})(?![.,;:!?‚Ä¶])", re.IGNORECASE) out = pattern.sub(rf"\1{pause_token}", out) return out def apply_cheerful_guide_style(text: str) -> str: content = insert_guidance_pauses(text) return f"{CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT}\n\n{content}" utils/splitter.py python# utils/splitter.py def split_text(text: str, char_limit: int = 6000): """Chunk by characters, splitting on sentence boundaries where possible.""" import re sents = re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\s+', text.strip()) chunks, cur = [], "" for s in sents: if len(cur) + len(s) + 1 > char_limit and cur: chunks.append(cur.strip()) cur = s else: cur = (cur + " " + s).strip() if cur: chunks.append(cur) return chunks utils/mixer.py python# utils/mixer.py from pydub import AudioSegment, effects import os, random AMBIENT_DIR = "ambient" def normalize_audio(seg: AudioSegment, target_dbfs: float = -14.0) -> AudioSegment: seg = effects.normalize(seg) change = target_dbfs - seg.dBFS return seg.apply_gain(change) def overlay_ambience(segment: AudioSegment, ambient_key: str | None, volume_db: int = -26) -> AudioSegment: if not ambient_key: return segment path = os.path.join(AMBIENT_DIR, f"{ambient_key}.mp3") if not os.path.exists(path): return segment amb = AudioSegment.from_mp3(path) + volume_db if len(amb) < len(segment): loops = len(segment) // len(amb) + 1 amb = amb * loops amb = amb[:len(segment)] return segment.overlay(amb) def binauralize(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.2, delay_ms: int = 35) -> AudioSegment: left = seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)) right = seg.pan(abs(pan_amount)).apply_gain(-1).fade_in(delay_ms) return left.overlay(right) def widen(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.3) -> AudioSegment: return seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)).overlay(seg.pan(abs(pan_amount))) Shared model chooser (drop-in helper) Create utils/model_select.py to centralize the ‚Äúbest model first‚Äù logic and Hugging Face fallback. python# utils/model_select.py import os from openai import OpenAI OPENAI_KEY = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY") HF_KEY = os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY") HF_MODEL = os.getenv("HF_TTS_MODEL", "suno/bark-small") PREFERRED = ["gpt-4o-tts", "gpt-4o-audio", "gpt-4o-mini-tts"] def choose_best_openai_model(): client = OpenAI(api_key=OPENAI_KEY) try: models = [m.id for m in client.models.list().data] for name in PREFERRED: if name in models: return client, name except Exception: pass return None, None def can_use_hf(): return bool(HF_KEY) def hf_params(): return HF_KEY, HF_MODEL thinketh_tts_adaptive.py python#!/usr/bin/env python3 """ Adaptive emotional audiobook generator (Cheerful Guide style). Prefers OpenAI gpt-4o-tts, falls back to HF Bark if needed. """ import os from pathlib import Path from dotenv import load_dotenv from docx import Document from pydub import AudioSegment from utils.splitter import split_text from utils.mixer import normalize_audio from utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style from utils.model_select import choose_best_openai_model, can_use_hf, hf_params import requests load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) VOICE = os.getenv("OPENAI_TTS_VOICE", "verse") OUT_DIR = Path("output_adaptive"); OUT_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True) BITRATE = "320k" def get_source(): path = input("üìÇ Please enter the path to your .docx source file:\n‚Üí ").strip() if not os.path.exists(path): raise FileNotFoundError("Source file not found.") return path def read_chapters(docx_path: str): doc = Document(docx_path) chapters, cur_t, cur_b = [], None, [] for p in doc.paragraphs: t = p.text.strip() if not t: continue if t.isupper() and len(t.split()) < 10: if cur_t: chapters.append((cur_t.title(), "\n".join(cur_b))) cur_t, cur_b = t, [] else: cur_b.append(t) if cur_t: chapters.append((cur_t.title(), "\n".join(cur_b))) print(f"üé¨ Found {len(chapters)} chapters.") return chapters def openai_tts(client, model, text, voice, out_path: Path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) # Use non-streaming create with response_format resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) def hf_bark_tts(text, out_path: Path): key, model = hf_params() headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HF TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def synthesize_chunk(text, tmp_path: Path): client, model = choose_best_openai_model() if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, text, VOICE, tmp_path) elif can_use_hf(): hf_bark_tts(text, tmp_path) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS model available (OpenAI or HF).") def main(): src = get_source() chapters = read_chapters(src) for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): out_file = OUT_DIR / f"{idx:02d}-{title.lower().replace(' ','-')}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping: {out_file.name}") continue print(f"üîä Synthesizing: {title}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(0) chunks = split_text(body, 6000) # safe chunking for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks, 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp) combined += AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) + AudioSegment.silent(400) combined = normalize_audio(combined, target_dbfs=-14.0).fade_in(300).fade_out(500) combined.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=BITRATE) print(f"üéß Saved: {out_file}") print(f"\n‚úÖ All done ‚Üí {OUT_DIR}") if __name__ == "__main__": main() thinketh_tts_asmr.py python#!/usr/bin/env python3 """ ASMR whisper edition with cheerful-guide affect, ambient option, binaural widening, 320 kbps mastering. """ import os, random from pathlib import Path from dotenv import load_dotenv from docx import Document from pydub import AudioSegment, effects from utils.splitter import split_text from utils.mixer import overlay_ambience, binauralize, normalize_audio from utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style from utils.model_select import choose_best_openai_model, can_use_hf, hf_params import requests load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) VOICE = os.getenv("OPENAI_TTS_VOICE_ASMR", "cove") OUT_DIR = Path("output_asmr"); OUT_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True) BITRATE = "320k" AMBIENTS = ["forest","rain","wind","fire","temple"] def get_source(): path = input("üìÇ Please enter the path to your .docx source file:\n‚Üí ").strip() if not os.path.exists(path): raise FileNotFoundError("Source file not found.") return path def openai_tts(client, model, text, voice, out_path: Path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) def hf_bark_tts(text, out_path: Path): key, model = hf_params() headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HF TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def synthesize_chunk(text, tmp_path: Path): client, model = choose_best_openai_model() if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, text, VOICE, tmp_path) elif can_use_hf(): hf_bark_tts(text, tmp_path) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS model available (OpenAI or HF).") def main(): src = get_source() doc = Document(src) text = "\n".join(p.text for p in doc.paragraphs if p.text.strip()) chunks = split_text(text, 6000) print("üåô Generating ASMR edition‚Ä¶") amb_key = random.choice(AMBIENTS) combined = AudioSegment.silent(500) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunks, 1): tmp = OUT_DIR / f"asmr_part{i}.mp3" synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, amb_key, volume_db=-28) seg = binauralize(seg) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(500) combined = normalize_audio(combined, target_dbfs=-16.0).fade_in(1500).fade_out(1500) out_mp3 = OUT_DIR / "asmr_thinketh_cheerful_guide.mp3" combined.export(out_mp3, format="mp3", bitrate=BITRATE) print(f"‚ú® ASMR track exported ‚Üí {out_mp3}") if __name__ == "__main__": main() thinketh_tts_scripty.py python#!/usr/bin/env python3 """ Cinematic hybrid edition: - cheerful-guide affect baked in - dynamic voice rotation - ambient overlays per chapter - widening, fades, -14 LUFS target, 320 kbps mastering """ import os, random from pathlib import Path from dotenv import load_dotenv from docx import Document from pydub import AudioSegment from utils.splitter import split_text from utils.mixer import overlay_ambience, widen, normalize_audio from utils.styles import apply_cheerful_guide_style from utils.model_select import choose_best_openai_model, can_use_hf, hf_params import requests load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) VOICES_ROTATION = ["verse","alloy","cove"] OUT_DIR = Path("output_scripty"); OUT_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True) BITRATE = "320k" CHAPTER_AMBIENT = { "Foreword": "temple", "Thought And Character": "fire", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "rain", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "forest", "Thought And Purpose": "wind", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "fire", "Visions And Ideals": "temple", "Serenity": "forest", } def get_source(): path = input("üìÇ Please enter the path to your .docx source file:\n‚Üí ").strip() if not os.path.exists(path): raise FileNotFoundError("Source file not found.") return path def openai_tts(client, model, text, voice, out_path: Path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) def hf_bark_tts(text, out_path: Path): key, model = hf_params() headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HF TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def synthesize_chunk(text, tmp_path: Path, voice: str): client, model = choose_best_openai_model() if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, text, voice, tmp_path) elif can_use_hf(): hf_bark_tts(text, tmp_path) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS model available (OpenAI or HF).") def parse_chapters(docx_path: str): doc = Document(docx_path) chapters, cur_t, cur_b = [], None, [] for p in doc.paragraphs: t = p.text.strip() if not t: continue if t.isupper() and len(t.split()) < 10: if cur_t: chapters.append((cur_t.title(), "\n".join(cur_b))) cur_t, cur_b = t, [] else: cur_b.append(t) if cur_t: chapters.append((cur_t.title(), "\n".join(cur_b))) print(f"üé¨ Found {len(chapters)} chapters.") return chapters def main(): src = get_source() chapters = parse_chapters(src) master = AudioSegment.silent(500) for i, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): voice = VOICES_ROTATION[i % len(VOICES_ROTATION)] amb_key = CHAPTER_AMBIENT.get(title, random.choice(list(CHAPTER_AMBIENT.values()))) out_ch = OUT_DIR / f"{i:02d}-{title.lower().replace(' ','-')}.mp3" if out_ch.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping: {out_ch.name}") continue print(f"üéôÔ∏è {title} ‚Üí voice {voice} | ambience {amb_key}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(250) for j, chunk in enumerate(split_text(body, 6000), 1): tmp = OUT_DIR / f"{i:02d}_part{j}.mp3" synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp, voice) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, amb_key, volume_db=-26) seg = widen(seg, pan_amount=0.28) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(700) combined = normalize_audio(combined, target_dbfs=-14.0).fade_in(1200).fade_out(1200) combined.export(out_ch, format="mp3", bitrate=BITRATE) master += combined + AudioSegment.silent(1500) master_out = OUT_DIR / "cinematic_master_cheerful_guide.mp3" master = normalize_audio(master, target_dbfs=-14.0).fade_in(1600).fade_out(1800) master.export(master_out, format="mp3", bitrate=BITRATE) print(f"üèÅ Complete ‚Üí {master_out}") if __name__ == "__main__": main() Notes you shouldn‚Äôt ignore These scripts prefer gpt-4o-tts automatically via utils/model_select.py. If that exact model isn‚Äôt available to your key, they‚Äôll try gpt-4o-audio, then gpt-4o-mini-tts. If OpenAI fails altogether, they‚Äôll use Hugging Face Bark if HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY exists. All TTS calls inject the Cheerful Guide style, including micro-pauses after instruction phrases. Everything exports 320 kbps MP3, normalized to audiobook-friendly loudness, with fades and optional ambience. If you want me to repackage this as a new zip, I‚Äôll spit out the archive creator again. Otherwise, slap these files in and run like a civilized human with taste.

## üë§ Human

## ü§ñ ChatGPT

You want one updated, unique, self-contained Python script that does it all. Fine. Here‚Äôs a single file that: reads a DOCX or TXT, auto-picks the best OpenAI TTS it finds (prefers gpt-4o-tts), falls back to Hugging Face Bark if needed, embeds your Cheerful Guide style with smart micro-pauses, supports three modes via CLI: adaptive, asmr, cinematic, handles chunking, ambience, binaural/stereo polish, normalization, exports 320 kbps MP3 chapters and a master file, loads keys from ~/.env. Drop it anywhere and run. python#!/usr/bin/env python3 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*- """ scripty_tts_unified.py A single-file audiobook TTS engine with: - Auto model selection (OpenAI GPT-4o TTS preferred; HF Bark fallback) - Cheerful Guide narration style with micro-pauses after instructions - Three render modes: adaptive, asmr, cinematic - 320 kbps mastering, fades, optional ambience, stereo polish - Chapter parsing for DOCX; TXT supported as single chapter Usage examples: python scripty_tts_unified.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode adaptive python scripty_tts_unified.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode asmr --voice cove python scripty_tts_unified.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode cinematic --bitrate 320k Env: expects OPENAI_API_KEY in ~/.env; optional HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY for fallback. """ import os import re import json import argparse from pathlib import Path from typing import List, Tuple, Optional from dotenv import load_dotenv from pydub import AudioSegment, effects # Optional deps used lazily: # - openai (OpenAI SDK) # - python-docx (for .docx parsing) # - requests (HF fallback) # ========================= # Environment / Constants # ========================= load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) BITRATE_DEFAULT = "320k" TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT = -14.0 PREFERRED_OPENAI_TTS = [ "gpt-4o-tts", # first choice if you have access "gpt-4o-audio", # strong audio-capable model (naming varies by account) "gpt-4o-mini-tts" # last-resort OpenAI TTS ] AMBIENT_CHOICES = ["forest", "rain", "fire", "wind", "temple"] CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT = { "Foreword": "temple", "Thought And Character": "fire", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "rain", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "forest", "Thought And Purpose": "wind", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "fire", "Visions And Ideals": "temple", "Serenity": "forest", } CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT = ( "Narration style: a cheerful guide. " "Tone: friendly, clear, and reassuring. " "Pronunciation: clear, articulate, steady. " "Pacing: brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions to allow processing. " "Emotion: warm and supportive, with empathy and care. " "Voice: warm, upbeat, and reassuring, steady, confident cadence. " "Dialect: neutral and professional, friendly and approachable. " "Be positive and solution-oriented, focusing on next steps. " "If imperatives appear (e.g., turn right, cross the street, continue straight), add a short pause right after." ) PAUSE_KEYWORDS = [ "turn right", "turn left", "continue straight", "cross the street", "merge right", "merge left", "take the exit", "keep right", "keep left", "stop here", "slow down", "look both ways", "proceed with caution" ] # ========================= # Utility: text shaping # ========================= def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ‚Ä¶ ") -> str: out = text for phrase in PAUSE_KEYWORDS: pattern = re.compile(rf"({re.escape(phrase)})(?![.,;:!?‚Ä¶])", re.IGNORECASE) out = pattern.sub(rf"\1{pause_token}", out) return out def apply_cheerful_guide_style(text: str) -> str: content = insert_guidance_pauses(text) return f"{CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT}\n\n{content}" def split_sentences(text: str) -> List[str]: # simple sentence splitter; avoids external heavy deps return re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\s+', text.strip()) def chunk_text(text: str, char_limit: int = 6000) -> List[str]: sents = split_sentences(text) chunks, cur = [], "" for s in sents: piece = (s if cur == "" else " " + s) if len(cur) + len(piece) > char_limit and cur: chunks.append(cur.strip()) cur = s else: cur += piece if cur.strip(): chunks.append(cur.strip()) return chunks # ========================= # Utility: audio shaping # ========================= def normalize_audio(seg: AudioSegment, target_dbfs: float = TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT) -> AudioSegment: seg = effects.normalize(seg) change = target_dbfs - seg.dBFS return seg.apply_gain(change) def overlay_ambience(segment: AudioSegment, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], volume_db: int = -26) -> AudioSegment: if not ambient_key: return segment amb_path = ambient_dir / f"{ambient_key}.mp3" if not amb_path.exists(): return segment amb = AudioSegment.from_mp3(amb_path) + volume_db # loop to match length if len(amb) < len(segment): loops = len(segment) // len(amb) + 1 amb = amb * loops amb = amb[:len(segment)] return segment.overlay(amb) def binauralize(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.2, attenuate_db: float = -1.0) -> AudioSegment: left = seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)) right = seg.pan(abs(pan_amount)).apply_gain(attenuate_db) return left.overlay(right) def widen(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.28) -> AudioSegment: return seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)).overlay(seg.pan(abs(pan_amount))) # ========================= # Model selection # ========================= def choose_best_openai_tts(): """ Returns (client, model) or (None, None). """ try: from openai import OpenAI except Exception: return None, None key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY") if not key: return None, None client = OpenAI(api_key=key) try: available = [m.id for m in client.models.list().data] for name in PREFERRED_OPENAI_TTS: if name in available: return client, name # If no exact match, attempt heuristic pick of any tts-capable: for m in available: if "tts" in m or "audio" in m: return client, m except Exception: pass return None, None def hf_fallback_available(): return bool(os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY")) def hf_tts(text: str, out_path: Path, model: str = None): """ Minimal Bark fallback through HF Inference API. """ import requests key = os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY") model = model or os.getenv("HF_TTS_MODEL", "suno/bark-small") headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"Hugging Face TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def openai_tts(client, model: str, voice: str, text: str, out_path: Path): styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) # Some SDKs use response_format, others use format. Try response_format first. try: resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) return except Exception: # Fallback param name resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) # ========================= # Source parsing # ========================= def read_docx_chapters(path: Path) -> List[Tuple[str, str]]: from docx import Document doc = Document(str(path)) chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]] = [] cur_title, cur_body = None, [] for p in doc.paragraphs: t = (p.text or "").strip() if not t: continue if t.isupper() and len(t.split()) < 10: if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) cur_title, cur_body = t, [] else: cur_body.append(t) if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) return chapters def read_txt(path: Path) -> str: return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8") # ========================= # Rendering modes # ========================= def render_adaptive(source_text_or_chapters, out_dir: Path, voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): client, model = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) if isinstance(source_text_or_chapters, list): chapters = source_text_or_chapters else: chapters = [("Chapter", source_text_or_chapters)] for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{title.lower().replace(' ','-')}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") continue print(f"üîä Synthesizing: {title}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(0) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 6000), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, voice, chunk, tmp) elif hf_fallback_available(): hf_tts(chunk, tmp) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS engine available.") combined += AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) + AudioSegment.silent(400) final = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(300).fade_out(500) final.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üéß Saved: {out_file}") def render_asmr(full_text: str, out_path: Path, voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], bitrate: str): client, model = choose_best_openai_tts() tmp = out_path.with_name(out_path.stem + "_tmp.mp3") # single-output ASMR flow; can be extended to chapters if needed print("üåô Generating ASMR‚Ä¶") if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, voice, full_text, tmp) elif hf_fallback_available(): hf_tts(full_text, tmp) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS engine available.") seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, ambient_key or "forest", volume_db=-28) seg = binauralize(seg, pan_amount=0.2, attenuate_db=-1.0) seg = normalize_audio(seg, target_dbfs=-16.0).fade_in(1500).fade_out(1500) seg.export(out_path, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"‚ú® ASMR track exported ‚Üí {out_path}") def render_cinematic(chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]], out_dir: Path, voices: List[str], ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): client, model = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) master = AudioSegment.silent(500) for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): voice = voices[idx % len(voices)] amb_key = CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT.get(title, None) out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{title.lower().replace(' ','-')}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") # still add to master master += AudioSegment.from_mp3(out_file) + AudioSegment.silent(1000) continue print(f"üéôÔ∏è {title} ‚Üí voice {voice} | ambience {amb_key or 'none'}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(250) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 6000), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, voice, chunk, tmp) elif hf_fallback_available(): hf_tts(chunk, tmp) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS engine available.") seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, amb_key, volume_db=-26) if amb_key else seg seg = widen(seg, pan_amount=0.28) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(700) combined = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1200).fade_out(1200) combined.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) master += combined + AudioSegment.silent(1500) master_out = out_dir / "cinematic_master_cheerful_guide.mp3" master = normalize_audio(master, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1600).fade_out(1800) master.export(master_out, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üèÅ Complete ‚Üí {master_out}") # ========================= # CLI # ========================= def parse_args(): ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Unified audiobook TTS (Cheerful Guide).") ap.add_argument("--source", "-s", type=str, help="Path to .docx or .txt") ap.add_argument("--mode", "-m", type=str, default="adaptive", choices=["adaptive","asmr","cinematic"], help="Render mode") ap.add_argument("--voice", "-v", type=str, default=None, help="OpenAI voice: verse, cove, alloy, ash, etc.") ap.add_argument("--ambient-dir", type=str, default="ambient", help="Folder containing ambient .mp3s") ap.add_argument("--ambient", type=str, default=None, help="Force ambient key (forest/rain/fire/wind/temple); otherwise auto") ap.add_argument("--bitrate", type=str, default=BITRATE_DEFAULT, help="Output MP3 bitrate (e.g., 320k)") ap.add_argument("--out", type=str, default=None, help="Output directory override") return ap.parse_args() def main(): args = parse_args() source = Path(args.source) if args.source else Path(input("üìÇ Source .docx or .txt:\n‚Üí ").strip()) if not source.exists(): raise FileNotFoundError(f"Not found: {source}") ambient_dir = Path(args.ambient_dir) ambient_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True, parents=True) # Select default voice based on mode if not provided if args.voice: voice = args.voice else: voice = "verse" if args.mode in ("adaptive", "cinematic") else "cove" # Output directories per mode if args.out: out_dir = Path(args.out) else: out_dir = Path(f"output_{args.mode}") out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) if source.suffix.lower() == ".docx": chapters = read_docx_chapters(source) if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(chapters, out_dir, voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": # Join for full-length asmr; you can adjust to chapterized if desired full_text = "\n".join(body for _, body in chapters) out_file = out_dir / "asmr_thinketh_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(full_text, out_file, voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: render_cinematic(chapters, out_dir, voices=["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir=ambient_dir, bitrate=args.bitrate) else: # TXT: treat as single body text = read_txt(source) if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(text, out_dir, voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": out_file = out_dir / f"{source.stem}_asmr_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(text, out_file, voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: # fake single "chapter" to reuse cinematic flow render_cinematic([("Chapter", text)], out_dir, ["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir, args.bitrate) if __name__ == "__main__": main() What you get in one file: Auto OpenAI model detection with gpt-4o-tts preference, plus HF Bark fallback. Your Cheerful Guide persona injected into every request, with micro-pauses on instruction phrases. --mode adaptive|asmr|cinematic to switch styles without juggling scripts. Ambience support, stereo polish, 320 kbps mastering, chapter parsing for DOCX. Run it like a grown-up: bashpip install openai python-docx python-dotenv pydub requests python scripty_tts_unified.py --source "/Users/steven/Documents/Txt/AS-A-MAN-THINKETH-nonformat.docx" --mode cinematic --bitrate 320k If your account actually has the ‚Äúbest‚Äù TTS, it‚Äôll use it. If not, it fails gracefully to a decent open-source fallback instead of having a meltdown. You're welcome.

## üë§ Human

analyze and then update and improve

## ü§ñ ChatGPT

Alright, captain sunshine, I dug into your thinketh_tts_mine.zip and surprise: it mostly works, but it‚Äôs fragile in all the usual places. Token limits? Barely handled. Model names? Assumed. Errors and retries? Nope. Resume safety? Meh. Good news: I cleaned it up and handed you one upgraded, self-contained script that‚Äôs smarter, tougher, and actually nice to use. Below is a single drop-in replacement that: auto-selects the best TTS model you actually have (prefers gpt-4o-tts, gracefully falls back, or uses Hugging Face Bark if OpenAI isn‚Äôt available), injects your Cheerful Guide persona with micro-pauses after instruction phrases, token-aware chunking (rough estimator) so you stop smacking 400s, retries with exponential backoff on flaky 429/5xx responses, resume-safe: skips already-finished chunks and chapters, modes: adaptive, asmr, cinematic in one file, 320 kbps mastering, fades, ambience, stereo polish, interactive source or --source CLI. Paste it as scripty_tts_unified_v2.py and run. scripty_tts_unified_v2.py python#!/usr/bin/env python3 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*- """ scripty_tts_unified_v2.py All-in-one audiobook TTS engine with: - Model auto-selection (prefers OpenAI gpt-4o-tts; falls back to other tts/audio; then HF Bark) - Cheerful Guide persona with micro-pauses for imperative instructions - Token-aware chunking, retries, resume, 320 kbps mastering - Three modes: adaptive (chapter mp3s), asmr (single whisper master), cinematic (multi-voice + ambience) Usage: python scripty_tts_unified_v2.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode adaptive python scripty_tts_unified_v2.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode asmr --voice cove python scripty_tts_unified_v2.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode cinematic --bitrate 320k Requires: pip install openai python-docx python-dotenv pydub requests """ import os, re, time, json, random, argparse, math from pathlib import Path from typing import List, Tuple, Optional from dotenv import load_dotenv from pydub import AudioSegment, effects # lazy imports inside functions: # from openai import OpenAI # from docx import Document # import requests # ========================= # Env + constants # ========================= load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) BITRATE_DEFAULT = "320k" TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT = -14.0 PREFERRED_MODELS = [ "gpt-4o-tts", # first choice if permitted "gpt-4o-audio", # alt premium audio-capable "gpt-4o-mini-tts" # last resort ] CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT = ( "Narration style: a cheerful guide. " "Tone: friendly, clear, and reassuring. " "Pronunciation: clear, articulate, steady. " "Pacing: brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions to allow processing. " "Emotion: warm and supportive, with empathy and care. " "Voice: warm, upbeat, and reassuring, steady, confident cadence. " "Dialect: neutral and professional, friendly and approachable. " "Be positive and solution-oriented, focusing on next steps. " "If imperatives appear (e.g., turn right, cross the street, continue straight), add a short pause right after." ) PAUSE_KEYWORDS = [ "turn right", "turn left", "continue straight", "cross the street", "merge right", "merge left", "take the exit", "keep right", "keep left", "stop here", "slow down", "look both ways", "proceed with caution" ] AMBIENT_CHOICES = ["forest", "rain", "fire", "wind", "temple"] CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT = { "Foreword": "temple", "Thought And Character": "fire", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "rain", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "forest", "Thought And Purpose": "wind", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "fire", "Visions And Ideals": "temple", "Serenity": "forest", } # ========================= # Helpers: text shaping # ========================= def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ‚Ä¶ ") -> str: out = text for phrase in PAUSE_KEYWORDS: pattern = re.compile(rf"({re.escape(phrase)})(?![.,;:!?‚Ä¶])", re.IGNORECASE) out = pattern.sub(rf"\1{pause_token}", out) return out def apply_cheerful_guide_style(text: str) -> str: content = insert_guidance_pauses(text) return f"{CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT}\n\n{content}" def split_sentences(text: str) -> List[str]: return re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\s+', text.strip()) def approx_token_count(s: str) -> int: # crude but effective: ~4 chars/token return max(1, math.ceil(len(s) / 4)) def chunk_text(text: str, token_limit: int = 1800) -> List[str]: """Token-aware chunking. Keeps chunks under ~token_limit tokens.""" sents = split_sentences(text) chunks, cur = [], "" cur_tokens = 0 for s in sents: stoks = approx_token_count(s) if cur and (cur_tokens + stoks > token_limit): chunks.append(cur.strip()) cur, cur_tokens = s, stoks else: cur = (cur + " " + s).strip() if cur else s cur_tokens += stoks if cur: chunks.append(cur.strip()) return chunks def safe_name(name: str) -> str: return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-]+", "-", name.lower()).strip("-") # ========================= # Helpers: audio shaping # ========================= def normalize_audio(seg: AudioSegment, target_dbfs: float = TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT) -> AudioSegment: seg = effects.normalize(seg) change = target_dbfs - seg.dBFS return seg.apply_gain(change) def overlay_ambience(segment: AudioSegment, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], volume_db: int = -26) -> AudioSegment: if not ambient_key: return segment amb_path = ambient_dir / f"{ambient_key}.mp3" if not amb_path.exists(): return segment amb = AudioSegment.from_mp3(amb_path) + volume_db if len(amb) < len(segment): loops = len(segment) // len(amb) + 1 amb = amb * loops amb = amb[:len(segment)] return segment.overlay(amb) def binauralize(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.2, attenuate_db: float = -1.0) -> AudioSegment: left = seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)) right = seg.pan(abs(pan_amount)).apply_gain(attenuate_db) return left.overlay(right) def widen(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.28) -> AudioSegment: return seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)).overlay(seg.pan(abs(pan_amount))) # ========================= # Model selection + TTS # ========================= def choose_best_openai_tts(): """Return (client, model) or (None, None).""" try: from openai import OpenAI except Exception: return None, None key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY") if not key: return None, None client = OpenAI(api_key=key) try: available = [m.id for m in client.models.list().data] # Prefer explicit models for name in PREFERRED_MODELS: if name in available: return client, name # Otherwise grab any audio/tts-capable for m in available: mid = m.lower() if "tts" in mid or "audio" in mid: return client, m except Exception: pass return None, None def hf_fallback_available(): return bool(os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY")) def hf_tts(text: str, out_path: Path, model: Optional[str] = None): import requests key = os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY") model = model or os.getenv("HF_TTS_MODEL", "suno/bark-small") headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HF TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def _retry_backoff(attempt: int, base: float = 1.0, cap: float = 20.0): time.sleep(min(cap, base * (2 ** (attempt - 1)))) def openai_tts(client, model: str, voice: str, text: str, out_path: Path, max_retries: int = 5): """Robust TTS with retries and response_format fallback.""" styled = apply_cheerful_guide_style(text) last_err = None for attempt in range(1, max_retries + 1): try: # Try modern param resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) return except Exception as e1: last_err = e1 # Try legacy param once per attempt try: resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) return except Exception as e2: last_err = e2 _retry_backoff(attempt) raise RuntimeError(f"OpenAI TTS failed after {max_retries} attempts: {last_err}") # ========================= # Source parsing # ========================= def read_docx_chapters(path: Path) -> List[Tuple[str, str]]: from docx import Document doc = Document(str(path)) chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]] = [] cur_title, cur_body = None, [] for p in doc.paragraphs: t = (p.text or "").strip() if not t: continue if t.isupper() and len(t.split()) < 10: if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) cur_title, cur_body = t, [] else: cur_body.append(t) if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) return chapters def read_txt(path: Path) -> str: return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8") # ========================= # Renderers # ========================= def synthesize_chunk(text: str, tmp_path: Path, openai_pack, voice: str): client, model = openai_pack if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, voice, text, tmp_path) elif hf_fallback_available(): hf_tts(text, tmp_path) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS engine available (OpenAI or Hugging Face).") def render_adaptive(source_text_or_chapters, out_dir: Path, voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) chapters = source_text_or_chapters if isinstance(source_text_or_chapters, list) else [("Chapter", source_text_or_chapters)] for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{safe_name(title)}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") continue print(f"üîä Synthesizing: {title}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(0) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 1800), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp, openai_pack, voice) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(400) final = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(300).fade_out(500) final.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üéß Saved: {out_file}") def render_asmr(full_text: str, out_path: Path, voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() tmp = out_path.with_name(out_path.stem + "_tmp.mp3") print("üåô Generating ASMR‚Ä¶") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(full_text, tmp, openai_pack, voice) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, ambient_key or "forest", volume_db=-28) seg = binauralize(seg, pan_amount=0.2, attenuate_db=-1.0) seg = normalize_audio(seg, target_dbfs=-16.0).fade_in(1500).fade_out(1500) seg.export(out_path, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"‚ú® ASMR track exported ‚Üí {out_path}") def render_cinematic(chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]], out_dir: Path, voices: List[str], ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) master = AudioSegment.silent(500) for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): voice = voices[idx % len(voices)] amb_key = CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT.get(title, random.choice(AMBIENT_CHOICES)) out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{safe_name(title)}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") master += AudioSegment.from_mp3(out_file) + AudioSegment.silent(1000) continue print(f"üéôÔ∏è {title} ‚Üí voice {voice} | ambience {amb_key}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(250) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 1800), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp, openai_pack, voice) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, amb_key, volume_db=-26) seg = widen(seg, pan_amount=0.28) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(700) combined = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1200).fade_out(1200) combined.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) master += combined + AudioSegment.silent(1500) master_out = out_dir / "cinematic_master_cheerful_guide.mp3" master = normalize_audio(master, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1600).fade_out(1800) master.export(master_out, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üèÅ Complete ‚Üí {master_out}") # ========================= # CLI # ========================= def parse_args(): ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Unified audiobook TTS (Cheerful Guide).") ap.add_argument("--source", "-s", type=str, help="Path to .docx or .txt") ap.add_argument("--mode", "-m", type=str, default="adaptive", choices=["adaptive","asmr","cinematic"], help="Render mode") ap.add_argument("--voice", "-v", type=str, default=None, help="OpenAI voice: verse, cove, alloy, ash, etc.") ap.add_argument("--ambient-dir", type=str, default="ambient", help="Folder containing ambient .mp3s") ap.add_argument("--ambient", type=str, default=None, help="Force ambient key (forest/rain/fire/wind/temple); otherwise auto") ap.add_argument("--bitrate", type=str, default=BITRATE_DEFAULT, help="Output MP3 bitrate (e.g., 320k)") ap.add_argument("--out", type=str, default=None, help="Output directory override") return ap.parse_args() def main(): args = parse_args() source = Path(args.source) if args.source else Path(input("üìÇ Source .docx or .txt:\n‚Üí ").strip()) if not source.exists(): raise FileNotFoundError(f"Not found: {source}") ambient_dir = Path(args.ambient_dir) ambient_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True, parents=True) # Choose default voice per mode if not provided if args.voice: voice = args.voice else: voice = "verse" if args.mode in ("adaptive", "cinematic") else "cove" # Output directory out_dir = Path(args.out) if args.out else Path(f"output_{args.mode}") out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) if source.suffix.lower() == ".docx": chapters = read_docx_chapters(source) print(f"üé¨ Found {len(chapters)} chapters.") if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(chapters, out_dir, voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": full_text = "\n".join(body for _, body in chapters) out_file = out_dir / "asmr_thinketh_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(full_text, out_file, voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: render_cinematic(chapters, out_dir, voices=["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir=ambient_dir, bitrate=args.bitrate) else: text = read_txt(source) if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(text, out_dir, voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": out_file = out_dir / f"{safe_name(source.stem)}_asmr_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(text, out_file, voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: render_cinematic([("Chapter", text)], out_dir, ["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir, args.bitrate) if __name__ == "__main__": main() What I fixed, in plain English Model selection: Stops assuming unicorns. Picks the best model you actually have. If OpenAI says no, it falls back to HF Bark automatically. Token-aware chunking: Rough token estimator so you don‚Äôt exceed limits. No more 2000-token tantrums. Retries + backoff: Those weird 429s and 5xx errors? It politely retries with exponential nap time. Resume safety: Re-running won‚Äôt double-synthesize everything. It uses existing chunk files where possible. Ambience + polish: ASMR and cinematic get subtle ambience and stereo widening. Normalized loudness for audiobook sanity. Cheerful Guide persona: Consistent style + micro-pauses after instructions. Run it like this: bashpip install openai python-docx python-dotenv pydub requests python scripty_tts_unified_v2.py --source "/Users/steven/Documents/Txt/AS-A-MAN-THINKETH-nonformat.docx" --mode cinematic --bitrate 320k If you want to keep your three-script setup too, fine; but if you just want one file that behaves like a competent adult, this is it.

Broad Park Avenue, Ilfracombe, England üéß Saved: output_adaptive/01-james-allen-broad-park-avenue-ilfracombe-england.mp3 üîä Synthesizing: Thought And Character üéß Saved: output_adaptive/02-thought-and-character.mp3 üîä Synthesizing: Effect Of Thought On Circumstances üéß Saved: output_adaptive/03-effect-of-thought-on-circumstances.mp3 üîä Synthesizing: Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body üéß Saved: output_adaptive/04-effect-of-thought-on-health-and-the-body.mp3 üîä Synthesizing: Thought And Purpose üéß Saved: output_adaptive/05-thought-and-purpose.mp3 üîä Synthesizing: The Thought-Factor In Achievement

## ü§ñ ChatGPT

Alright, here‚Äôs what went sideways and how I fixed it like an adult who‚Äôs tired of hearing TTS mispronounce ‚ÄúIlfracombe.‚Äù What happened in your run You got 9 chapters because the parser treated the signature block JAMES ALLEN. / BROAD PARK AVENUE, / ILFRACOMBE, / ENGLAND as a brand-new chapter. Two of those lines are ALL CAPS, which tripped your ‚Äúheading‚Äù heuristic. The narration affect applied uniformly. That‚Äôs fine for IKEA manuals, not for a philosophical text. Foreword needs warm welcome; ‚ÄúAchievement‚Äù needs conviction; ‚ÄúSerenity‚Äù should basically breathe. Pauses were generic. Verse/quotes didn‚Äôt get enough air. Addresses got read like headlines. Not your vibe. What I changed Smarter chapter parsing Keeps the signature block inside the Foreword instead of becoming Chapter 2. Heading detection is stricter: ALL CAPS plus a whitelist; short ALL CAPS that look like addresses are not headings. Per-chapter narration styles Each chapter gets its own style preset layered on top of your ‚ÄúCheerful Guide‚Äù baseline. Examples: Foreword: warm, inviting Thought & Character: reflective, measured Achievement: energized, confident Serenity: calm, ASMR-adjacent Voice mapping per chapter Uses verse for general narration, alloy for firm chapters (Achievement, Purpose), cove for Serenity and Health. You can override via CLI if you must. Quote/verse handling Detects short poetic lines and adds longer pauses and softer attack around them so it stops sounding like a traffic report. Safer chunking Keeps your ~1800 token aim, but prioritizes splitting between stanza/paragraph boundaries where possible. Resume-safe and minimal re-render You only need to delete the broken file(s) and rerun. It won‚Äôt trash the good chapters. Drop-in replacement: scripty_tts_unified_v3.py Paste this as a new file and use it instead of v2. It keeps your 320 kbps mastering, ambience, retries, etc., and adds the good stuff above. python#!/usr/bin/env python3 # -*- coding: utf-8 -*- """ scripty_tts_unified_v3.py Smarter chapter parsing, per-chapter narration styles, voice mapping, gentle verse handling, resume-safe rendering, 320 kbps mastering. Usage: python scripty_tts_unified_v3.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode adaptive python scripty_tts_unified_v3.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode cinematic python scripty_tts_unified_v3.py --source "/path/book.docx" --mode asmr --voice cove """ import os, re, time, json, random, argparse, math from pathlib import Path from typing import List, Tuple, Optional from dotenv import load_dotenv from pydub import AudioSegment, effects # lazy imports inside functions: # from openai import OpenAI # from docx import Document # import requests load_dotenv(os.path.expanduser("~/.env")) BITRATE_DEFAULT = "320k" TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT = -14.0 PREFERRED_MODELS = ["gpt-4o-tts", "gpt-4o-audio", "gpt-4o-mini-tts"] AMBIENT_CHOICES = ["forest", "rain", "fire", "wind", "temple"] # ---------- Global baseline style ---------- CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT = ( "Narration style: a cheerful guide. " "Tone: friendly, clear, reassuring. " "Pronunciation: clear, articulate, steady. " "Pacing: brief, purposeful pauses after key instructions to allow processing. " "Emotion: warm and supportive, with empathy and care. " "Voice: warm, upbeat, reassuring, steady, confident cadence. " "Dialect: neutral and professional, friendly and approachable. " "Be positive and solution-oriented, focusing on next steps. " "If imperatives appear (e.g., turn right, cross the street, continue straight), " "add a short pause right after." ) # ---------- Per-chapter style overlays ---------- CHAPTER_STYLE = { "Foreword": "Welcome the listener with gentle warmth; reassure and set context briefly.", "Thought And Character": "Reflective and measured; emphasize cause-and-effect with calm clarity.", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "Supportive, instructive; keep cadence steady to highlight logical steps.", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "Soothing, health-focused reassurance; soften any harshness.", "Thought And Purpose": "Focused and motivating; clear calls to action with confident cadence.", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "Energized confidence; purposeful emphasis on effort and responsibility.", "Visions And Ideals": "Lightly inspirational; broaden imagery with gentle uplift.", "Serenity": "Quiet, calm, and restorative; allow more air between lines and clauses." } # ---------- Voice per chapter ---------- CHAPTER_VOICE = { "Foreword": "verse", "Thought And Character": "verse", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "verse", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "cove", "Thought And Purpose": "alloy", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "alloy", "Visions And Ideals": "verse", "Serenity": "cove", } # ---------- Ambience per chapter ---------- CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT = { "Foreword": "temple", "Thought And Character": "fire", "Effect Of Thought On Circumstances": "rain", "Effect Of Thought On Health And The Body": "forest", "Thought And Purpose": "wind", "The Thought-Factor In Achievement": "fire", "Visions And Ideals": "temple", "Serenity": "forest", } PAUSE_KEYWORDS = [ "turn right", "turn left", "continue straight", "cross the street", "merge right", "merge left", "take the exit", "keep right", "keep left", "stop here", "slow down", "look both ways", "proceed with caution" ] # ---------- Text shaping ---------- def insert_guidance_pauses(text: str, pause_token: str = " ‚Ä¶ ") -> str: out = text for phrase in PAUSE_KEYWORDS: pattern = re.compile(rf"({re.escape(phrase)})(?![.,;:!?‚Ä¶])", re.IGNORECASE) out = pattern.sub(rf"\1{pause_token}", out) return out def soften_verse(text: str) -> str: """ Heuristic: if a block looks like verse (short lines, many breaks), add subtle spacing and softeners before/after to give it air. """ lines = text.splitlines() short_lines = [ln for ln in lines if 0 < len(ln.strip()) <= 60] if len(short_lines) >= 3 and len(short_lines) >= len(lines) * 0.5: return f"(gentle pause) {text} (gentle pause)" return text def apply_style_for_chapter(text: str, chapter: str) -> str: base = CHEERFUL_GUIDE_PROMPT overlay = CHAPTER_STYLE.get(chapter, "") content = soften_verse(insert_guidance_pauses(text)) return f"{base}\n\nChapter intent: {overlay}\n\n{content}" def split_sentences(text: str): return re.split(r'(?<=[.!?])\s+', text.strip()) def approx_tokens(s: str) -> int: return max(1, math.ceil(len(s) / 4)) def chunk_text(text: str, token_limit: int = 1800) -> List[str]: sents = re.split(r"(\n{2,})", text) # preserve paragraph breaks as split points chunks, cur, cur_tokens = [], "", 0 for piece in sents: toks = approx_tokens(piece) if cur and (cur_tokens + toks > token_limit): chunks.append(cur.strip()) cur, cur_tokens = piece, toks else: cur = (cur + piece) if cur else piece cur_tokens += toks if cur.strip(): chunks.append(cur.strip()) return chunks def safe_name(name: str) -> str: return re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9\-]+", "-", name.lower()).strip("-") # ---------- Audio shaping ---------- def normalize_audio(seg: AudioSegment, target_dbfs: float = TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT) -> AudioSegment: seg = effects.normalize(seg) change = target_dbfs - seg.dBFS return seg.apply_gain(change) def overlay_ambience(segment: AudioSegment, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], volume_db: int = -26) -> AudioSegment: if not ambient_key: return segment amb_path = ambient_dir / f"{ambient_key}.mp3" if not amb_path.exists(): return segment amb = AudioSegment.from_mp3(amb_path) + volume_db if len(amb) < len(segment): loops = len(segment) // len(amb) + 1 amb = amb * loops amb = amb[:len(segment)] return segment.overlay(amb) def binauralize(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.2, attenuate_db: float = -1.0) -> AudioSegment: left = seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)) right = seg.pan(abs(pan_amount)).apply_gain(attenuate_db) return left.overlay(right) def widen(seg: AudioSegment, pan_amount: float = 0.28) -> AudioSegment: return seg.pan(-abs(pan_amount)).overlay(seg.pan(abs(pan_amount))) # ---------- Model selection + TTS ---------- def choose_best_openai_tts(): try: from openai import OpenAI except Exception: return None, None key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY") if not key: return None, None client = OpenAI(api_key=key) try: available = [m.id for m in client.models.list().data] for name in PREFERRED_MODELS: if name in available: return client, name for m in available: mid = m.lower() if "tts" in mid or "audio" in mid: return client, m except Exception: pass return None, None def hf_fallback_available(): return bool(os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY")) def hf_tts(text: str, out_path: Path, model: Optional[str] = None): import requests key = os.getenv("HUGGINGFACE_API_KEY") model = model or os.getenv("HF_TTS_MODEL", "suno/bark-small") headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {key}"} resp = requests.post( f"https://api-inference.huggingface.co/models/{model}", headers=headers, json={"inputs": text}, stream=True, timeout=300 ) if resp.status_code != 200: raise RuntimeError(f"HF TTS error: {resp.text}") with open(out_path, "wb") as f: for chunk in resp.iter_content(8192): f.write(chunk) def _retry_backoff(attempt: int, base: float = 1.0, cap: float = 20.0): time.sleep(min(cap, base * (2 ** (attempt - 1)))) def openai_tts(client, model: str, voice: str, text: str, out_path: Path, chapter: str, max_retries: int = 5): styled = apply_style_for_chapter(text, chapter) last_err = None for attempt in range(1, max_retries + 1): try: resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, response_format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) return except Exception as e1: last_err = e1 try: resp = client.audio.speech.create( model=model, voice=voice, input=styled, format="mp3" ) out_path.write_bytes(resp.read()) return except Exception as e2: last_err = e2 _retry_backoff(attempt) raise RuntimeError(f"OpenAI TTS failed after {max_retries} attempts: {last_err}") # ---------- Source parsing (improved) ---------- ADDRESS_TOKENS = {"BROAD", "AVENUE", "ILFRACOMBE", "ENGLAND", "PARK"} KNOWN_HEADINGS = { "FOREWORD", "THOUGHT AND CHARACTER", "EFFECT OF THOUGHT ON CIRCUMSTANCES", "EFFECT OF THOUGHT ON HEALTH AND THE BODY", "THOUGHT AND PURPOSE", "THE THOUGHT-FACTOR IN ACHIEVEMENT", "VISIONS AND IDEALS", "SERENITY", } def is_probable_heading(t: str) -> bool: if not t: return False if t.upper() in KNOWN_HEADINGS: return True # Reject address-like ALL CAPS if t.isupper(): words = set(re.findall(r"[A-Z]+", t)) if words & ADDRESS_TOKENS: return False # reasonable short heading return len(t.split()) <= 8 return False def read_docx_chapters(path: Path) -> List[Tuple[str, str]]: from docx import Document doc = Document(str(path)) chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]] = [] cur_title, cur_body = None, [] for p in doc.paragraphs: t = (p.text or "").strip() if not t: continue if is_probable_heading(t): if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) cur_title, cur_body = t, [] else: # Special case: signature block lines get appended to current body if t.upper() in {"JAMES ALLEN.", "BROAD PARK AVENUE,", "ILFRACOMBE,", "ENGLAND"}: cur_body.append(t) else: cur_body.append(t) if cur_title: chapters.append((cur_title.title(), "\n".join(cur_body))) # Final guard: if a tiny "address chapter" slipped through, merge back to previous merged: List[Tuple[str, str]] = [] for title, body in chapters: if title.title() in {"James Allen.", "Broad Park Avenue,", "Ilfracombe,", "England"}: if merged: prev_t, prev_b = merged[-1] merged[-1] = (prev_t, prev_b + "\n" + title + "\n" + body) else: merged.append((title, body)) else: merged.append((title, body)) return merged def read_txt(path: Path) -> str: return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8") # ---------- Renderers ---------- def synthesize_chunk(text: str, tmp_path: Path, openai_pack, voice: str, chapter_title: str): client, model = openai_pack if client and model: openai_tts(client, model, voice, text, tmp_path, chapter_title) elif hf_fallback_available(): hf_tts(text, tmp_path) else: raise RuntimeError("No TTS engine available (OpenAI or Hugging Face).") def render_adaptive(chapters_or_text, out_dir: Path, default_voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) chapters = chapters_or_text if isinstance(chapters_or_text, list) else [("Chapter", chapters_or_text)] for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): voice = CHAPTER_VOICE.get(title, default_voice) out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{safe_name(title)}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") continue print(f"üîä Synthesizing: {title}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(0) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 1800), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp, openai_pack, voice, title) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(400) final = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(300).fade_out(500) final.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üéß Saved: {out_file}") def render_asmr(full_text: str, out_path: Path, voice: str, ambient_dir: Path, ambient_key: Optional[str], bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() tmp = out_path.with_name(out_path.stem + "_tmp.mp3") chapter_title = "Serenity" print("üåô Generating ASMR‚Ä¶") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(full_text, tmp, openai_pack, voice, chapter_title) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, ambient_key or "forest", volume_db=-28) seg = binauralize(seg, pan_amount=0.2, attenuate_db=-1.0) seg = normalize_audio(seg, target_dbfs=-16.0).fade_in(1500).fade_out(1500) seg.export(out_path, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"‚ú® ASMR track exported ‚Üí {out_path}") def render_cinematic(chapters: List[Tuple[str, str]], out_dir: Path, voices: List[str], ambient_dir: Path, bitrate: str): openai_pack = choose_best_openai_tts() out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) master = AudioSegment.silent(500) for idx, (title, body) in enumerate(chapters): voice = CHAPTER_VOICE.get(title, voices[idx % len(voices)]) amb_key = CHAPTER_TO_AMBIENT.get(title, random.choice(AMBIENT_CHOICES)) out_file = out_dir / f"{idx:02d}-{safe_name(title)}.mp3" if out_file.exists(): print(f"‚úÖ Skipping (exists): {out_file.name}") master += AudioSegment.from_mp3(out_file) + AudioSegment.silent(1000) continue print(f"üéôÔ∏è {title} ‚Üí voice {voice} | ambience {amb_key}") combined = AudioSegment.silent(250) for i, chunk in enumerate(chunk_text(body, 1800), 1): tmp = out_file.with_name(f"{out_file.stem}_part{i}.mp3") if tmp.exists(): seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) else: synthesize_chunk(chunk, tmp, openai_pack, voice, title) seg = AudioSegment.from_mp3(tmp) seg = overlay_ambience(seg, ambient_dir, amb_key, volume_db=-26) seg = widen(seg, pan_amount=0.28) combined += seg + AudioSegment.silent(700) combined = normalize_audio(combined, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1200).fade_out(1200) combined.export(out_file, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) master += combined + AudioSegment.silent(1500) master_out = out_dir / "cinematic_master_cheerful_guide.mp3" master = normalize_audio(master, TARGET_DBFS_DEFAULT).fade_in(1600).fade_out(1800) master.export(master_out, format="mp3", bitrate=bitrate) print(f"üèÅ Complete ‚Üí {master_out}") # ---------- CLI ---------- def parse_args(): ap = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Unified audiobook TTS with per-chapter style.") ap.add_argument("--source", "-s", type=str, help="Path to .docx or .txt") ap.add_argument("--mode", "-m", type=str, default="adaptive", choices=["adaptive","asmr","cinematic"]) ap.add_argument("--voice", "-v", type=str, default=None, help="OpenAI voice override (verse, cove, alloy, ash, etc.)") ap.add_argument("--ambient-dir", type=str, default="ambient") ap.add_argument("--ambient", type=str, default=None, help="Force ambient key (forest/rain/fire/wind/temple); else per-chapter") ap.add_argument("--bitrate", type=str, default=BITRATE_DEFAULT) ap.add_argument("--out", type=str, default=None) return ap.parse_args() def main(): args = parse_args() source = Path(args.source) if args.source else Path(input("üìÇ Source .docx or .txt:\n‚Üí ").strip()) if not source.exists(): raise FileNotFoundError(f"Not found: {source}") ambient_dir = Path(args.ambient_dir); ambient_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True, parents=True) default_voice = args.voice or ("verse" if args.mode in ("adaptive","cinematic") else "cove") out_dir = Path(args.out) if args.out else Path(f"output_{args.mode}"); out_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True) if source.suffix.lower() == ".docx": chapters = read_docx_chapters(source) print(f"üé¨ Found {len(chapters)} chapters.") if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(chapters, out_dir, default_voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": full_text = "\n".join(body for _, body in chapters) out_file = out_dir / "asmr_thinketh_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(full_text, out_file, default_voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: render_cinematic(chapters, out_dir, voices=["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir=ambient_dir, bitrate=args.bitrate) else: text = read_txt(source) if args.mode == "adaptive": render_adaptive(text, out_dir, default_voice, ambient_dir, args.bitrate) elif args.mode == "asmr": out_file = out_dir / f"{safe_name(source.stem)}_asmr_cheerful_guide.mp3" render_asmr(text, out_file, default_voice, ambient_dir, args.ambient, args.bitrate) else: render_cinematic([("Chapter", text)], out_dir, ["verse","alloy","cove"], ambient_dir, args.bitrate) if __name__ == "__main__": main() How to fix your current outputs fast Save the script above as scripty_tts_unified_v3.py. Delete the bogus ‚Äúaddress chapter‚Äù file: bashrm output_adaptive/01-james-allen-broad-park-avenue-ilfracombe-england.mp3 Re-run adaptive: csspython scripty_tts_unified_v3.py --source "/Users/steven/Downloads/Compressed/thinketh_tts_mine/AS-A-MAN-THINKETH-nonformat.docx" --mode adaptive You should get 8 clean chapters, with the signature left inside the Foreword. If you want stricter calm in ‚ÄúSerenity,‚Äù run: csspython scripty_tts_unified_v3.py --source "...docx" --mode cinematic --voice verse The script still uses cove for ‚ÄúSerenity,‚Äù but --voice lets you force a single voice if you‚Äôre feeling dictatorial. You get per-chapter affect, better parsing, and your audiobook stops sounding like a cheerful GPS reading a postage label.
